## Australia - family Visa
### Source: Australia_family.txt
VISA TYPE: Australian Family Visas - Child, Remaining Relative, NZ Citizen Family
COUNTRY: Australia
SOURCE: https://immi.homeaffairs.gov.au/visas/getting-a-visa/visa-listing/

---CHUNK:2---
affairs.gov.au/visas/getting-a-visa/visa-listing/
LAST UPDATED: 2024
=== VISA SUBCLASSES OVERVIEW ===
SUBCLASS 445 - DEPENDENT CHILD VISA (TEMPORARY):
- Purpose: Allows child to stay temporarily while parent's permanent Partner visa (100/801) is processed
- Stay: Temporary, until decision on parent's permanent visa
- Cost: From AUD 3,235
- Apply: Paper application only
- Requirement: Child's parent must hold temporary Partner visa (309/820) or dependent child visa
SUBCLASS 101 - CHILD VISA (OFFSHORE):

---CHUNK:3---
child visa
SUBCLASS 101 - CHILD VISA (OFFSHORE):
- Purpose: Child outside Australia moves to Australia to live with parent(s)
- Stay: Permanent residence
- Cost: From AUD 3,235
- Apply: Paper application only; must be OUTSIDE Australia when applying and when decided
- Sponsor: Eligible parent who is Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen
SUBCLASS 802 - CHILD VISA (ONSHORE):
- Purpose: Child already in Australia stays permanently with parent(s)
- Stay: Permanent residence
- Cost: From AUD 3,235

---CHUNK:4---
Stay: Permanent residence
- Cost: From AUD 3,235
- Apply: Paper application only; must be INSIDE Australia when applying and when decided
- Sponsor: Eligible parent who is Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen
SUBCLASS 102 - ADOPTION VISA:
- Purpose: Child adopted (or in process of adoption) outside Australia moves to Australia with adoptive parent
- Stay: Permanent residence
- Cost: From AUD 3,235
- Apply: Paper application only; child must be OUTSIDE Australia

---CHUNK:5---
application only; child must be OUTSIDE Australia
- Requirement: Adoption must comply with Hague Convention or bilateral arrangement
SUBCLASS 115 - REMAINING RELATIVE VISA (OFFSHORE):
- Purpose: Person moves to Australia to be with their only close family members
- Stay: Permanent residence
- Cost: From AUD 5,280
- Apply: Paper application; must be OUTSIDE Australia when applying and when decided
- Queue wait: Up to 50 years (Other Family Visa Queue)
SUBCLASS 835 - REMAINING RELATIVE VISA (ONSHORE):

---CHUNK:6---
SUBCLASS 835 - REMAINING RELATIVE VISA (ONSHORE):
- Purpose: Person already in Australia stays to be with only close family members
- Stay: Permanent residence
- Cost: From AUD 5,280
- Apply: Paper application; must be INSIDE Australia when applying and when decided
- Queue wait: Up to 50 years (Other Family Visa Queue)
SUBCLASS 461 - NEW ZEALAND CITIZEN FAMILY RELATIONSHIP VISA:
- Purpose: Non-NZ citizen who is member of family unit of NZ citizen lives/works in Australia
- Stay: Temporary, up to 5 years (renewable)
- Cost: From AUD 445

---CHUNK:7---
y, up to 5 years (renewable)
- Cost: From AUD 445
- Apply: Online or paper; can apply inside OR outside Australia
- Rights: Live, work, study in Australia; travel freely while valid
=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
CHILD VISAS (101, 802, 445):
□ Child must be under 18, OR 18-25 and financially dependent, OR 18+ with disability preventing self-support
□ Child must be single (not married/in de facto relationship)
□ Child must be sponsored by eligible parent (Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen)

---CHUNK:8---
arent (Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen)
□ Parent must have legal right to determine child's residence (custody/guardianship)
□ For subclass 802/445: Child must hold eligible substantive visa if applying onshore
□ Health and character requirements apply
ADOPTION VISA (102):
□ Child must be under 18 at time of application
□ Adoption must be full/legal adoption (not de facto or customary)
□ Adoption must comply with Hague Convention or bilateral arrangement with Australia

---CHUNK:9---
onvention or bilateral arrangement with Australia
□ Adoptive parent must be Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen
□ At least one adoptive parent must be settled in Australia
□ Health and character requirements apply
REMAINING RELATIVE VISAS (115, 835):
□ Applicant must be 18+ years old
□ Applicant must have NO near relatives (spouse, children, parents, siblings) living outside Australia
□ "Near relatives" in Australia must be Australian citizen/PR/eligible NZ citizen
□ Must be sponsored by eligible relative in Australia

---CHUNK:10---
st be sponsored by eligible relative in Australia
□ Must meet Balance of Family Test implications (all/near relatives in Australia)
□ Health and character requirements apply
□ Queue wait: Up to 50 years (non-contributory family queue)
NEW ZEALAND CITIZEN FAMILY RELATIONSHIP (461):
□ Applicant must NOT be a New Zealand citizen
□ Applicant must be member of family unit of NZ citizen who holds Special Category Visa (subclass 444)
- Family unit includes: spouse/de facto partner, dependent child, or dependent relative

---CHUNK:11---
o partner, dependent child, or dependent relative
□ NZ citizen family member must be living in Australia or intending to live in Australia
□ Applicant must meet health and character requirements
□ No sponsorship required, but must demonstrate family relationship
=== SPONSORSHIP REQUIREMENTS ===
SPONSOR MUST:
□ Be Australian citizen, permanent resident, or eligible New Zealand citizen
□ Be 18+ years old
□ Provide Assurance of Support (AoS) for most family visas (financial bond ~AUD 10,000-14,000)

---CHUNK:12---
family visas (financial bond ~AUD 10,000-14,000)
□ Agree to provide financial/emotional support for first 2 years after grant
□ Not be barred from sponsoring (previous sponsorship failures, criminal history)
ASSURANCE OF SUPPORT (AoS):
- Required for: Child visas (101/802), Remaining Relative visas (115/835)
- Not required for: Subclass 461 (NZ Citizen Family)
- Amount: ~AUD 10,400 for primary applicant, ~AUD 4,500 for each additional adult
- Held by government for 2 years; refunded if no social security claims made

---CHUNK:13---
years; refunded if no social security claims made
=== HEALTH & CHARACTER REQUIREMENTS ===
HEALTH:
- Medical examination required for all permanent family visa applicants
- Must be done by Bupa Medical Visa Services panel physician
- Includes chest x-ray (age 11+), HIV test (age 15+), full medical (age 75+)
- Results valid for 12 months
CHARACTER:
- Police certificate required from every country lived in 12+ months during past 10 years (since age 16)
- Must declare ALL criminal history, including spent convictions and minor offences

---CHUNK:14---
y, including spent convictions and minor offences
- False/misleading information can result in refusal + 3-year ban
=== APPLICATION PROCESS ===
PAPER APPLICATIONS (MOST FAMILY VISAS):
1. Download correct form from ImmiAccount:
- Form 47CH: Child visa (101/802)
- Form 47OA: Adoption visa (102)
- Form 47SH: Remaining Relative visa (115/835)
2. Complete form + gather supporting documents
3. Mail application to specified address with payment
4. Await acknowledgment + case officer assignment
5. Respond to any requests for additional information

---CHUNK:15---
espond to any requests for additional information
6. Wait for decision (processing times vary significantly by queue)
ONLINE APPLICATION (SUBCLASS 461 ONLY):
1. Create ImmiAccount: https://online.immi.gov.au
2. Complete NZ Citizen Family Relationship visa application
3. Upload supporting documents (relationship proof, NZ citizen's visa status)
4. Pay application charge (AUD 445) by credit card
5. Await decision (typically faster than paper applications)
=== FEES (2024) ===
- Child visas (101/802/445): AUD 3,235
- Adoption visa (102): AUD 3,235

---CHUNK:16---
/445): AUD 3,235
- Adoption visa (102): AUD 3,235
- Remaining Relative visas (115/835): AUD 5,280
- NZ Citizen Family Relationship (461): AUD 445
- Assurance of Support bond (if required): ~AUD 10,400 primary + AUD 4,500 per additional adult
- Payment: Credit card (online) or bank cheque/money order (paper applications)
=== PROCESSING TIMES (GUIDE ONLY) ===
- Child visas (101/802): Check visa processing time guide tool; typically 12-24 months
- Adoption visa (102): Varies by country of adoption; typically 12-36 months

---CHUNK:17---
es by country of adoption; typically 12-36 months
- Remaining Relative visas (115/835): Up to 50 years (Other Family Visa Queue)
- NZ Citizen Family Relationship (461): Typically 3-6 months
=== VISA CONDITIONS (IF GRANTED) ===
CHILD VISAS:
- Full work and study rights upon grant
- Access to Medicare (if eligible)
- Pathway to citizenship after 4 years permanent residence
REMAINING RELATIVE VISAS:
- Full work and study rights
- Access to Medicare and social security (after waiting periods)

---CHUNK:18---
icare and social security (after waiting periods)
- Pathway to citizenship after 4 years permanent residence
SUBCLASS 461 (NZ CITIZEN FAMILY):
- Full work and study rights in Australia
- Travel freely while visa valid
- Must maintain family relationship with NZ citizen holder of subclass 444
- Does NOT lead directly to permanent residence (separate application required)
=== PATHWAY TO CITIZENSHIP ===
- After holding permanent family visa for 4 years (including 12 months as PR), may apply for Australian citizenship by conferral

---CHUNK:19---
may apply for Australian citizenship by conferral
- Must meet residence requirements, character test, and citizenship test
- Children under 16 may be included in parent's citizenship application
=== RESTRICTIONS & RISKS ===
✗ Remaining Relative visas have extreme queue waits (up to 50 years); consider alternative visas if urgent
✗ Child must remain dependent (financially/emotionally) for eligibility; independence may affect status
✗ Adoption must be legally recognized by Australia; informal/customary adoptions not accepted

---CHUNK:20---
tralia; informal/customary adoptions not accepted
✗ Subclass 461 is temporary; must reapply every 5 years or transition to another visa for permanence
✗ All family visas require genuine relationship; sham relationships result in refusal + 3-year ban
✗ Overstaying or breaching visa conditions affects future Australian immigration applications

## Australia - Student Visa
### Source: Australia_Student.txt
VISA TYPE: Student Visa Subclass 500
COUNTRY: Australia

YPE: Student Visa Subclass 500
COUNTRY: Australia
SOURCE: https://immi.homeaffairs.gov.au/visas/getting-a-visa/visa-listing/student-500
LAST UPDATED: 2024
=== OVERVIEW ===
- Participate in eligible course of study in Australia
- Stay: Up to 6 years, aligned with course duration
- Cost: From AUD 2,000 (exemptions for Pacific Island/Timor-Leste citizens from 22 March 2025)
- Apply: Online via ImmiAccount, inside or outside Australia
- Processing: Prioritized per Ministerial Direction 111 (before 14 Nov 2025) or 115 (on/after 14 Nov 2025)

---CHUNK:22---
before 14 Nov 2025) or 115 (on/after 14 Nov 2025)
=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Apply online in or outside Australia
□ Be enrolled in CRICOS-registered course and hold valid Confirmation of Enrolment (CoE) at decision time
□ Hold Overseas Student Health Cover (OSHC) for entire stay (or qualify for exemption)
□ Be 6 years or older
□ Prove approved welfare arrangements if under 18
□ If applying inside Australia: Hold eligible substantive visa (not Bridging E, not subject to condition 8503)
□ Meet Genuine Student (GS) requirement

---CHUNK:23---
ion 8503)
□ Meet Genuine Student (GS) requirement
□ Meet financial capacity requirements
□ Meet English language proficiency requirements
□ Meet health and character requirements
=== GENUINE STUDENT (GS) REQUIREMENT ===
MUST DEMONSTRATE GENUINE INTENTION TO STUDY:
- Current knowledge of chosen course and education provider
- Academic history and logical progression to selected course
- Value of Australian qualification to future employment/home country
- Personal circumstances: ties to home country, immigration history

---CHUNK:24---
tances: ties to home country, immigration history
- No primary intention to use student visa as migration pathway
=== FINANCIAL CAPACITY REQUIREMENTS ===
PROOF OF FUNDS (ONE OF THE FOLLOWING):
OPTION 1 - MONEY DEPOSITS:
- Sufficient funds for: travel + 12 months living costs (AUD 24,505) + 12 months tuition
- Additional for dependents: Partner AUD 8,574/year, Child AUD 3,670/year
- Funds must be held with financial institution for 3+ months
OPTION 2 - ANNUAL INCOME:

---CHUNK:25---
stitution for 3+ months
OPTION 2 - ANNUAL INCOME:
- Parent/partner annual income: AUD 72,465 (single student) or AUD 84,540 (with dependents)
- Supported by official tax documents/employment letters
OPTION 3 - LOAN/SCHOLARSHIP:
- Loan from financial institution covering required amounts
- Government scholarship/financial support letter
=== ENGLISH LANGUAGE REQUIREMENTS ===
MINIMUM SCORES BY COURSE LEVEL:
- Higher Education (Bachelor/Master): IELTS 6.0 overall (no band <5.5) OR PTE 50, TOEFL iBT 78

---CHUNK:26---
.0 overall (no band <5.5) OR PTE 50, TOEFL iBT 78
- Vocational Education (VET): IELTS 5.5 overall (no band <5.0) OR PTE 42, TOEFL iBT 46
- ELICOS: IELTS 5.0 overall OR equivalent
- Schools: Provider assesses; no formal test required
EXEMPTIONS:
- Passport holders: UK, USA, Canada, New Zealand, Republic of Ireland
- 5+ years of study in English-speaking country
- Specific packaged courses with integrated English component
=== OVERSEAS STUDENT HEALTH COVER (OSHC) ===
MANDATORY REQUIREMENTS:

---CHUNK:27---
T HEALTH COVER (OSHC) ===
MANDATORY REQUIREMENTS:
- Must cover entire visa duration from arrival to departure
- Approved providers: Allianz, Bupa, Medibank, NIB, AHM
- Coverage includes: Hospital treatment, outpatient services, pharmaceuticals, emergency ambulance
- Exemptions: Students from countries with reciprocal healthcare agreements (Belgium, Norway, etc.)
=== WORK RIGHTS ===
DURING COURSE SESSIONS:
- Maximum 48 hours per fortnight (all employment combined)
- Work must not interfere with course attendance/progress

---CHUNK:28---
ust not interfere with course attendance/progress
DURING SCHEDULED BREAKS:
- Unlimited work hours permitted
SPECIAL CASES:
- Postgraduate research students: Unlimited work rights after course commencement
- Course work component: Work integral to course (e.g., internship) doesn't count toward limit
BREACHING WORK CONDITIONS MAY RESULT IN VISA CANCELLATION
=== CRICOS COURSE REQUIREMENT ===
- Course MUST be registered on Commonwealth Register of Institutions and Courses for Overseas Students (CRICOS)

---CHUNK:29---
utions and Courses for Overseas Students (CRICOS)
- Provider MUST be approved to enroll international students
- Verify course CRICOS code: https://cricos.education.gov.au
- CoE is invalid if course is cancelled or completed
=== VISA CONDITIONS (IF GRANTED) ===
8105 – WORK LIMITATION: Max 48 hours/fortnight during sessions; unlimited during breaks
8202 – MEET COURSE REQUIREMENTS: Maintain enrolment, attend classes, achieve satisfactory course progress
8501 – MAINTAIN HEALTH INSURANCE: Hold adequate OSHC for entire stay

---CHUNK:31---

TEMPORARY GRADUATE VISA (SUBCLASS 485) ELIGIBILITY:

- Bachelor/Master (coursework): 2-3 years

changes, course changes, or cessation of studies

✗ Cannot work more than 48 hours/fortnight during course sessions

✗ Cannot access most government benefits (welfare, unemployment)

course progress; failure may lead to cancellation

yment, family ties, community involvement, assets

COUNTRY: Australia

=== OVERVIEW ===
- Enables employers to address labour shortages by bringing in skilled workers
- Replaces previous Temporary Skill Shortage (Subclass 482) visa
- Two main streams: Core Skills & Specialist Skills
- Stay: Up to 4 years (Up to 5 years for Hong Kong passport holders)
- Cost: From AUD 3,210 (Visa Application Charge)
- Processing times: Check official tool; varies by occupation and country
=== STREAM 1: CORE SKILLS ===
ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA:

---CHUNK:52---
= STREAM 1: CORE SKILLS ===
ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA:
□ Be nominated by an approved sponsor to work in an occupation on the Core Skills Occupation List (CSOL)
□ Be paid at least the Core Skills Income Threshold (CSIT) OR Annual Market Salary Rate (AMSR), whichever is higher
□ Have at least 1 year relevant work experience in nominated occupation or related field
□ Have a relevant skills assessment if required for occupation
□ Meet minimum standards of English language proficiency (Competent English: IELTS 5.0 or equivalent)

---CHUNK:53---
ency (Competent English: IELTS 5.0 or equivalent)
□ Work only for sponsor or associated entity (unless exempt)
□ Meet health and character requirements

- AUD 73,150 per year (indexed annually)
- Must be met via cash salary (non-monetary benefits excluded)
OCCUPATION LIST:
- Core Skills Occupation List (CSOL)
- Covers most skilled occupations facing shortages
=== STREAM 2: SPECIALIST SKILLS ===
ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA:
□ Be nominated to work in an ANZSCO occupation listed in Major Groups 1, 2, 4, 5,

---CHUNK:54---
SCO occupation listed in Major Groups 1, 2, 4, 5, or 6 (excluding trades)
□ Be paid at least the Specialist Skills Income Threshold
□ Have at least 1 year relevant work experience in nominated occupation or related field

1. IRCC assesses sponsor eligibility first

4. Federal stage resumes for final PR decision

=== SUPER VISA ALTERNATIVE (PARENTS/GRANDPARENTS) ===
If sponsorship backlog is long, consider Super Visa:
- Multiple-entry visa valid up to 10 years
- Allows stays up to 5 years per entry
- Requirements: Child/grandchild in Canada meets income threshold, private medical insurance ($100k coverage), medical exam
- Faster processing; does not lead to PR directly but allows extended visits
=== POST-APPROVAL ===
- Sponsored person becomes permanent resident upon entry to Canada

---CHUNK:74---
n becomes permanent resident upon entry to Canada
- Sponsor's undertaking lasts 3 years from date PR is granted (for spouse/partner)
- Sponsored person has right to work, study, access healthcare immediately
- Conditional permanent residence (2-year cohabitation requirement) was removed in 2017
=== APPEAL RIGHTS ===

- Refusal was not due to inadmissibility (serious criminality, security, human rights violations), AND
- Sponsor is Canadian citizen or PR

---CHUNK:75---
lations), AND
- Sponsor is Canadian citizen or PR

S2 VISA (SHORT-TERM):

e of issue (depending on nationality/reciprocity)

ull-time study if course duration ≤ visa validity

may be permitted with PSB approval

=== OVERVIEW ===
- X1 Visa: For long-term study (>180 days) at recognized Chinese educational institutions

---CHUNK:133---
s) at recognized Chinese educational institutions
- X2 Visa: For short-term study (≤180 days), language courses, exchange programs
- X1 Visa holders must convert to Residence Permit within 30 days of entry
- Sponsored by Chinese educational institution; requires Admission Notice + JW201/JW202 Form
=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Hold passport valid for at least 6 months beyond intended study period, with at least 2 blank visa pages

---CHUNK:134---
ed study period, with at least 2 blank visa pages
□ Have formal admission offer from recognized Chinese educational institution (university, college, language school)
□ Possess JW201 Form (for Chinese Government Scholarship recipients) or JW202 Form (for self-funded students)
□ Demonstrate sufficient financial resources to cover tuition + living expenses in China
□ Pass health examination at authorized facility (for X1 Visa; report valid for 6 months)
□ Not have adverse immigration history with China or other countries
RECOGNIZED INSTITUTIONS:

---CHUNK:135---
China or other countries

- Universities under Ministry of Education: http://www.moe.gov.cn

- Language schools approved by local education bureaus
- Verify institution recognition before applying; unaccredited institutions cannot issue valid JW forms
QUALIFYING PROGRAMS:
✓ Bachelor's, Master's, PhD degrees at recognized universities
✓ Chinese language programs (semester/year-long) at university language centers

---CHUNK:136---
emester/year-long) at university language centers

NON-QUALIFYING PROGRAMS:
✗ Informal/unaccredited language schools or training centers
✗ Online/distance learning programs without physical presence in China
✗ Short-term tourism-style "study tours" without formal academic enrollment

during academic term; full-time during vacations

=== VISA VALIDITY & ENTRY RULES ===
VALIDITY PERIODS:
- Single-entry: Typically 3 months from date of issue
- Double-entry: Typically 6 months from date of issue
- Multiple-entry: 6 months, 1 year, 2 years, 5 years, or 10 years (based on nationality/reciprocity)
DURATION OF STAY PER ENTRY:
- Typically 30 days for most nationalities
- USA/Canada citizens: Often granted 60-90 days per entry
- Specified on visa sticker as "Duration of Each Stay: XX days"
ENTRY/EXIT REQUIREMENTS:

---CHUNK:173---
n of Each Stay: XX days"
ENTRY/EXIT REQUIREMENTS:
- Must enter China within visa validity period
- Must exit before "Duration of Each Stay" expires
- Overstaying results in fines, detention, deportation, future entry bans
EXTENSION OF STAY IN CHINA:
- L Visa generally NOT extendable within China except in exceptional circumstances (medical emergency, force majeure)
- Apply at local Exit-Entry Administration Bureau of Public Security at least 7 days before expiry
- Approval discretionary; not for routine tourism extension

---CHUNK:174---
discretionary; not for routine tourism extension
=== RESTRICTED AREAS & SPECIAL PERMITS ===
TIBET AUTONOMOUS REGION:
- Foreign tourists MUST obtain Tibet Travel Permit in addition to Chinese visa
- Apply via licensed travel agency in China; cannot apply independently
- Permit required for entry to Tibet by air, train, or road
OTHER RESTRICTED AREAS:
- Certain border regions (Xinjiang, Yunnan, Guangxi) may require additional permits
- Military zones, sensitive research areas: Access restricted; special authorization required

---CHUNK:175---
Access restricted; special authorization required
- Check with travel agency or local Public Security Bureau for region-specific requirements
=== MEDICAL & CHARACTER REQUIREMENTS ===
MEDICAL EXAMINATION:
- Not required for tourist visa applications under 180 days
- May be requested for longer stays or if applicant has declared medical conditions
YELLOW FEVER VACCINATION:
- Required if arriving from countries with risk of yellow fever transmission
- Must present International Certificate of Vaccination (ICVP) at entry

---CHUNK:176---
tional Certificate of Vaccination (ICVP) at entry
CHARACTER/SECURITY SCREENING:
- All applicants subject to security background checks
- Previous travel to sensitive regions, criminal history, or adverse immigration record may trigger additional scrutiny
- Full disclosure required; false statements can result in visa refusal + future ban
=== REFUSAL & REAPPLICATION ===
COMMON REFUSAL GROUNDS:
✗ Incomplete application or missing documents
✗ Passport validity <6 months or insufficient blank pages

---CHUNK:177---
rt validity <6 months or insufficient blank pages
✗ Insufficient proof of funds, unclear travel purpose, or implausible itinerary
✗ Previous Chinese visa violations (overstay, unauthorized work, illegal entry)
✗ Security concerns or adverse background checks
✗ Applicant of Pakistani origin (special clearance required)
REAPPLICATION GUIDELINES:
- Address specific refusal reason with stronger documentation
- Enhance itinerary, financial proof, or invitation letter as needed
- Wait at least 30 days before reapplying unless circumstances changed

---CHUNK:178---
ys before reapplying unless circumstances changed
- For security-related refusals: May require special clearance from Ministry of Foreign Affairs
=== OVERSTAY PENALTIES ===
CONSEQUENCES OF OVERSTAYING:
- Fine: CNY 500 per day of overstay (max CNY 10,000)
- Possible detention (5-15 days) for serious/extended overstay
- Deportation at applicant's expense
- Entry ban: 1 year to permanent, depending on overstay duration and circumstances
- Future Chinese visa applications will face additional scrutiny or refusal
VOLUNTARY DEPARTURE:

---CHUNK:179---
ditional scrutiny or refusal
VOLUNTARY DEPARTURE:
- If realize overstay before detection: Report to nearest Exit-Entry Administration Bureau immediately
- May receive reduced penalty vs. being caught at airport exit
- Still results in immigration record affecting future applications

## China - work Visa

=== OVERVIEW ===
- Z Visa: For foreigners taking up employment or commercial performance in China
- Single-entry visa valid for 30 days from entry; must convert to Residence Permit within 30 days
- Sponsored by Chinese employer; requires Work Permit Notice from Ministry of Human Resources and Social Security (MOHRSS) or State Administration of Foreign Experts Affairs (SAFEA)

---CHUNK:182---
Administration of Foreign Experts Affairs (SAFEA)
- Mandatory registration with local Public Security Bureau within 24 hours of arrival
=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
APPLICANT MUST:
□ Have valid job offer/employment contract from Chinese employer registered to hire foreigners
□ Possess bachelor's degree or higher OR 2+ years relevant work experience (for most categories)
□ Be aged 18-60 (men) or 18-55 (women); exceptions for high-level talent
□ Pass health examination at authorized facility (report valid for 6 months)

---CHUNK:183---
t authorized facility (report valid for 6 months)
□ Have no criminal record in home country or China
□ Not be of Pakistani origin or hold Pakistani passport without special clearance (case-by-case)

✓ Executives, managers, technical experts assigned to Chinese entity

s, performers, athletes with commercial contracts

✗ Routine administrative/clerical staff without specialized skills
✗ Short-term consultants (<90 days; may use M/Business Visa)
✗ Self-employed freelancers serving Chinese clients (requires different authorization)
✗ Volunteers, interns without formal employment contract and Work Permit

=== WORK PERMIT CATEGORIES ===
CHINA CLASSIFIES FOREIGN WORKERS INTO THREE CATEGORIES:
CATEGORY A (HIGH-LEVEL TALENT):
- Eligibility: Senior executives, PhD holders, high-salary earners (≥2x local average), award winners, entrepreneurs
- Benefits: Fast-track Work Permit processing, longer validity (up to 5 years), family dependents eligible for longer permits

---CHUNK:194---
s), family dependents eligible for longer permits
- Documentation: Enhanced proof of achievements, awards, publications, patents
CATEGORY B (PROFESSIONAL TALENT):
- Eligibility: Bachelor's degree + 2 years experience, mid-level professionals, teachers, skilled technicians
- Standard processing timeline and validity (typically 1 year)
- Most common category for foreign employees
CATEGORY C (OTHER FOREIGN WORKERS):
- Eligibility: Seasonal workers, interns, short-term contractors (subject to quotas/restrictions)

---CHUNK:195---
term contractors (subject to quotas/restrictions)
- More stringent approval process; limited validity (≤1 year)
- Subject to labor market testing and quota controls
=== RESIDENCE PERMIT VALIDITY & RENEWAL ===
INITIAL VALIDITY:
- Typically 1 year, matching Work Permit validity
- Multiple-entry allowed; holder can travel in/out of China freely during validity
RENEWAL PROCESS:
- Apply at local Exit-Entry Administration Bureau at least 30 days before expiry
- Required documents:
- Valid passport and current Residence Permit

---CHUNK:196---
ts:
- Valid passport and current Residence Permit
- Renewed Work Permit from employer
- Updated health examination report (if required; typically every 1-2 years)
- Temporary Registration Form of Accommodation
- Employer's updated business license + foreigner employment registration
- Processing: 7-15 working days; applicant may stay in China during processing with acknowledgment receipt
- Renewal granted in 1-year increments; high-level talent (Category A) may receive 2-5 year renewals
=== FAMILY DEPENDENTS ===
ELIGIBILITY TO SPONSOR FAMILY:

---CHUNK:197---
ILY DEPENDENTS ===
ELIGIBILITY TO SPONSOR FAMILY:
- Z Visa/Residence Permit holders CAN sponsor spouse and unmarried children under 18 for S1/S2 Visa
- Dependents receive visa validity matching primary holder's Residence Permit
DEPENDENT VISA TYPES:
- S1 Visa: For long-term stay (>180 days); convert to Residence Permit within 30 days of entry
- S2 Visa: For short-term visits (≤180 days); no conversion required
DEPENDENT RIGHTS:
- Spouse: May study or engage in unpaid activities; cannot work without separate Work Permit

---CHUNK:198---
ivities; cannot work without separate Work Permit
- Children: Can enroll in Chinese schools; cannot work without authorization
- All dependents: Must register with local police within 24 hours of arrival; apply for Residence Permit if staying >180 days
=== TAX & COMPLIANCE OBLIGATIONS ===
INCOME TAX:
- Foreign employees are tax residents if stay in China exceeds 183 days in a calendar year
- Must obtain Tax Identification Number from local tax bureau
- Employer typically withholds Individual Income Tax (IIT); file annual tax reconciliation

---CHUNK:199---
Income Tax (IIT); file annual tax reconciliation
SOCIAL INSURANCE:
- Foreign employees in China generally required to contribute to social insurance (pension, medical, unemployment, work injury, maternity)
- Exemptions possible under bilateral social security agreements (e.g., with Germany, South Korea, Canada)
- Contribution rates vary by city; typically 10-20% of salary shared between employer/employee
LABOR LAW COMPLIANCE:
- Employment must comply with Chinese Labor Contract Law: minimum wage, working hours (max 44 hrs/week),

---CHUNK:200---
w: minimum wage, working hours (max 44 hrs/week), leave entitlements
- Foreign employees have same rights as Chinese employees under most labor statutes
- Disputes resolved via local labor arbitration committees
=== VISA/PERMIT CANCELLATION & EXIT PROCEDURES ===
EMPLOYMENT TERMINATION:
- If employment ends before permit expiry: Employer must cancel Work Permit and notify authorities within 10 days
- Residence Permit holder has 30-day grace period to:
- Secure new employment and transfer Work Permit sponsorship, OR

---CHUNK:201---
ployment and transfer Work Permit sponsorship, OR
- Change visa status (e.g., to S2/Tourist Visa), OR
- Depart China
EXIT CLEARANCE:
- No formal exit visa required for Residence Permit holders
- Ensure Work Permit cancellation and tax clearance before departure
- Carry passport with Residence Permit when exiting; may be asked for proof of employment/tax compliance
=== REFUSAL & REAPPLICATION ===
COMMON REFUSAL GROUNDS:
✗ Work Permit Notice invalid, expired, or from unregistered employer
✗ Qualifications not meeting Category A/B/C requirements

---CHUNK:202---
fications not meeting Category A/B/C requirements
✗ Health examination showing disqualifying conditions (infectious diseases, mental health concerns)
✗ Criminal record or adverse immigration history
✗ Incomplete documentation or inconsistent information
REAPPLICATION GUIDELINES:
- Address specific refusal reason: Secure valid Work Permit Notice, enhance qualification documentation, clarify employer credentials
- For health-related refusals: Obtain second medical opinion at authorized facility

---CHUNK:203---
ain second medical opinion at authorized facility
- Wait at least 30 days before reapplying unless circumstances changed significantly

- If no visa required: Enter France, apply for residence permit within 3 months
- Residence permit type: "Carte de séjour - membre de famille de citoyen UE/EEE/Suisse"
ADVANTAGES UNDER EU LAW:
- Faster processing (typically 1-3 months)

=== TAX & COMPLIANCE OBLIGATIONS ===
INCOME TAX:
- Employment Visa holders are tax residents if stay in India exceeds 182 days in a financial year (Apr-Mar)
- Must obtain Permanent Account Number (PAN) from Income Tax Department
- Employer typically deducts TDS (Tax Deducted at Source); file annual income tax return

lgium, Germany, France, Netherlands, Switzerland)

=== VISA CANCELLATION & EXIT PROCEDURES ===
EMPLOYMENT TERMINATION:

---CHUNK:394---
ION & EXIT PROCEDURES ===
EMPLOYMENT TERMINATION:
- If employment ends before visa expiry: Employer must notify FRRO/FRO within 7 days
- Visa holder has 30-day grace period to:
- Secure new employment and transfer visa sponsorship, OR
- Change visa status (e.g., to Tourist Visa), OR
- Depart India
EXIT CLEARANCE:
- No formal exit visa required for Employment Visa holders
- Ensure FRRO registration is up-to-date before departure
- Carry Employment Visa, passport, and Registration Certificate when exiting

✗ Qualifications/skills deemed readily available in Indian labor market
✗ Incomplete documentation from employer or applicant
✗ Previous Indian visa violations or adverse immigration history
✗ Security concerns related to sector, employer, or applicant background

- Address specific refusal reason: Increase salary offer, enhance skills documentation, clarify employer credentials

---CHUNK:396---
kills documentation, clarify employer credentials

=== OVERVIEW ===
Singapore offers several passes for family members of foreign professionals, entrepreneurs, and Singapore Citizens/Permanent Residents (SC/PR).

---CHUNK:410---

MAIN FAMILY PASS TYPES:

2. Long-Term Visit Pass (LTVP): For common-law spouses, step-children, handicapped children (>21), parents of EP holders, or family of SC/PR.
3. LTVP+ (Enhanced): For spouses of Singapore Citizens with stable income; offers longer validity and work rights.

---CHUNK:411---
e income; offers longer validity and work rights.

□ Hold a valid Employment Pass (EP), S Pass, or EntrePass.
□ Earn a fixed monthly salary of at least SGD 6,000 (higher for older applications).
□ Work for a well-established, reputable firm in Singapore.
ELIGIBLE FAMILY MEMBERS:
- Legally married spouse.

---CHUNK:412---
LIGIBLE FAMILY MEMBERS:
- Legally married spouse.
- Unmarried children under 21 years old (including legally adopted children).

- Required for foreigners accepted into approved full-time educational institutions in Singapore

=== OVERVIEW ===
South Korea offers several family-based residence visas depending on relationship to Korean citizen or foreign resident:
- F-1: Visiting/Temporary Stay (short-term family visits)

---CHUNK:477---
isiting/Temporary Stay (short-term family visits)
- F-2: Long-term residence (for spouses/children of Korean citizens or permanent residents)
- F-3: Dependent Visa (for family of foreign residents on E/D visas)
- F-4: Overseas Korean Visa (for ethnic Koreans with foreign citizenship)
- F-5: Permanent Residence (after meeting long-term residence criteria)
- F-6: Marriage Immigrant Visa (for foreign spouses of Korean citizens)
This file focuses on F-3 (Dependent) and F-6 (Marriage Immigrant) as most common for family reunification.

---CHUNK:478---
migrant) as most common for family reunification.

□ Accommodation in Korea must meet minimum standards

□ Completed visa application form

---CHUNK:479---

=== TAX & COMPLIANCE OBLIGATIONS ===
INCOME TAX:
- Foreign employees are tax residents if stay in Korea exceeds 183 days in a calendar year

- Employer typically withholds income tax; file annual tax return (May each year)
SOCIAL INSURANCE:

---CHUNK:558---
nual tax return (May each year)
SOCIAL INSURANCE:
- Foreign employees generally required to contribute to National Pension, Health Insurance, Employment Insurance, Industrial Accident Compensation
- Exemptions possible under bilateral social security agreements (e.g., with USA, Canada, Australia, UK, Germany)
- Contribution rates: ~9% of salary shared between employer/employee
LABOR LAW COMPLIANCE:
- Employment must comply with Korean Labor Standards Act: minimum wage, working hours (max 52 hrs/week), leave entitlements

rking hours (max 52 hrs/week), leave entitlements

- Disputes resolved via local labor committees or courts

- Secure new employment and transfer visa sponsorship, OR
- Change visa status (e.g., to tourist visa), OR
- Depart Korea

---CHUNK:560---
tourist visa), OR
- Depart Korea

- No formal exit visa required for ARC holders

PENSION REFUND:
- Foreign employees who leave Korea permanently may apply for National Pension refund
- Apply at National Pension Service within 5 years of departure
- Refund amount: Contributions made by employee (employer portion not refundable)

---CHUNK:561---
ade by employee (employer portion not refundable)

=== TAX & COMPLIANCE OBLIGATIONS ===
INCOME TAX:
- Foreign employees are tax residents if stay in Thailand exceeds 180 days in a calendar year
- Must obtain Tax ID from Revenue Department
- Employer typically withholds Personal Income Tax (PIT); file annual tax return (March each year)
- Tax rates: Progressive 5-35% based on income
SOCIAL SECURITY:

---CHUNK:649---
rogressive 5-35% based on income
SOCIAL SECURITY:
- Foreign employees generally required to contribute to Social Security Fund (if employer has 1+ Thai employees)
- Contribution: 5% of salary (capped at THB 750/month) shared between employer/employee
- Benefits: Healthcare, maternity, disability, death, pension
LABOR LAW COMPLIANCE:
- Employment must comply with Thai Labor Protection Act: minimum wage, working hours (max 48 hrs/week), leave entitlements
- Foreign employees have same rights as Thai employees under most labor statutes

---CHUNK:650---
ights as Thai employees under most labor statutes
- Disputes resolved via local labor courts or mediation
=== VISA/WORK PERMIT CANCELLATION & EXIT PROCEDURES ===
EMPLOYMENT TERMINATION:
- If employment ends before Work Permit expiry: Employer must cancel Work Permit within 7 days
- Visa holder has 24-hour grace period to depart Thailand OR change visa status
- Failure to depart/change status may result in overstay penalties
EXIT CLEARANCE:
- No formal exit visa required for Work Permit holders

formal exit visa required for Work Permit holders

=== OVERVIEW ===
- Expatriate residents with valid UAE residence permit can sponsor family members for residence visas

---CHUNK:655---
00/month OR AED 3,000/month + valid accommodation
- Sponsored family members receive residence visas linked to sponsor's visa validity (except parents: yearly visas)

- Profession type no longer a barrier to family sponsorship eligibility
=== SPONSOR ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
SPONSOR MUST:
□ Hold valid UAE residence permit/visa (not under cancellation process)

---CHUNK:656---
ss OR AED 3,000 gross + valid accommodation proof

MANDATORY FOR SPONSORED MEMBERS AGED 18+:

=== CANCELLATION & GRACE PERIOD ===
WHEN SPONSOR'S VISA IS CANCELLED:
- Dependents' visas automatically cancelled simultaneously
- 6-month grace period from cancellation date for dependents to:

---CHUNK:676---
period from cancellation date for dependents to:
- Obtain new sponsorship (new employer, family member, or investor visa)
- Change status to tourist visa and depart UAE
- Apply for Golden Visa or other long-term residence if eligible
CONSEQUENCES OF EXPIRING GRACE PERIOD:
- Overstay fines accrue: AED 125 first day, AED 25 each subsequent day
- Potential entry ban (6 months to permanent) for excessive overstay
- Future UAE visa applications face additional scrutiny
VOLUNTARY CANCELLATION OF DEPENDENT VISA:

---CHUNK:677---
crutiny
VOLUNTARY CANCELLATION OF DEPENDENT VISA:
- Sponsor can cancel dependent visa anytime via ICP/GDRFA portal
- Dependent must depart UAE within 30 days of cancellation or change status
- Deposit refund processed after dependent departure confirmation
SPONSOR RESPONSIBILITY:
- If sponsor fails to renew or cancel dependent visa upon expiry, sponsor may be liable for fines
- Fines for late renewal: Similar to overstay fines (AED 100-200/day after grace period)

- Emirates ID validity matches Golden Visa duration (5 or 10 years)
- Renewal process begins 30 days before expiry via ICP smart services
=== FAMILY SPONSORSHIP RIGHTS ===
ELIGIBLE DEPENDENTS:
- Spouse (legally married)
- Children (any age, including adult children)
- Parents (under specific conditions: financial dependency proof, accommodation)

---CHUNK:705---
tions: financial dependency proof, accommodation)
- Unlimited domestic helpers (separate application process)
DEPENDENT VISA DETAILS:
- Validity matches primary Golden Visa holder's duration
- Dependents receive residence permits enabling study, healthcare access
- Dependents can travel in/out of UAE with primary holder or independently
WORK RIGHTS FOR DEPENDENTS:
- Spouses: Can work in UAE but require separate work permit or Letter of Consent (if eligible under MOM rules)
- Adult children: Must obtain own work visa/permit for employment

---CHUNK:706---
: Must obtain own work visa/permit for employment
- Domestic helpers: Work rights limited to household duties for sponsoring family
=== RENEWAL PROCESS ===
ELIGIBILITY FOR RENEWAL:
- Must continue to meet original category requirements:
- Investors: Maintain investment threshold
- Entrepreneurs: Business remains operational and innovative
- Talents: Continue practicing in approved field with endorsements
- Students: Maintain academic standing if still studying
- No criminal record or immigration violations during visa validity

---CHUNK:707---
rd or immigration violations during visa validity
- Valid passport (6+ months remaining at renewal application)
RENEWAL STEPS:
1. Submit renewal application via ICP/GDRFA portal 30-90 days before expiry
2. Provide updated supporting documents (e.g., updated bank statements, employment letter, business license)
3. Complete medical examination if required (typically every 5 years)
4. Pay renewal fees (similar structure to initial issuance)
5. Receive renewed visa sticker + updated Emirates ID
=== VISA CANCELLATION CONDITIONS ===

---CHUNK:708---
Emirates ID
=== VISA CANCELLATION CONDITIONS ===
GOLDEN VISA MAY BE CANCELLED IF:
✗ Holder obtains residence in another country and abandons UAE residency
✗ Holder is convicted of serious crime or poses security threat to UAE
✗ Fraudulent documents or misrepresentation discovered during validity period
✗ Investor category: Investment withdrawn or falls below AED 2 million threshold
✗ Talent category: No longer practicing in approved field or losing ministry endorsements

---CHUNK:709---
in approved field or losing ministry endorsements
✗ Student category: Discontinued studies or failed to maintain required academic standards
✗ Violation of UAE laws or immigration regulations
CONSEQUENCES OF CANCELLATION:
- 30-day grace period to either rectify status or depart UAE
- Sponsored dependents' visas cancelled simultaneously
- Future UAE visa applications may face additional scrutiny or refusal
- Potential fines or penalties depending on violation nature
=== TRANSITION TO CITIZENSHIP ===
CURRENT POLICY:

---CHUNK:710---
=== TRANSITION TO CITIZENSHIP ===
CURRENT POLICY:
- Golden Visa is a long-term residence permit, NOT a direct pathway to UAE citizenship
- UAE citizenship is granted through separate, highly selective process (Royal Decree)
- Long-term residency via Golden Visa may strengthen future citizenship consideration but is not guaranteed
ALTERNATIVE PATHWAYS TO CITIZENSHIP:
- Naturalization: Typically requires 30 years continuous residence (reduced for certain categories like scientists, artists)

---CHUNK:711---
for certain categories like scientists, artists)
- Marriage to UAE national: Possible pathway with specific conditions and approval
- Exceptional contribution: Scientists, artists, investors may be considered for citizenship via special Royal Decree
- Note: Citizenship decisions are at discretion of UAE leadership; no automatic entitlement
=== COMPLIANCE & RESPONSIBILITIES ===
GOLDEN VISA HOLDER MUST:
- Maintain eligibility criteria throughout visa validity
- Renew visa before expiry to maintain legal status

---CHUNK:712---
Renew visa before expiry to maintain legal status
- Notify authorities of address changes, passport renewals, family status changes
- Comply with all UAE laws and regulations
- Ensure sponsored dependents also comply with visa conditions
PENALTIES FOR NON-COMPLIANCE:
- Visa cancellation and deportation for serious violations
- Fines for overstaying or working without proper authorization
- Future entry bans for fraudulent applications or criminal activity

=== VISA-EXEMPT & VISA-ON-ARRIVAL CONTEXT ===
WHO DOES NOT NEED THIS VISA:

---CHUNK:736---
ustralia, EU, Japan, South Korea, Singapore, etc.
- Select nationalities eligible for 90-day visa-on-arrival (non-extendable): Mexico, Seychelles, etc.

- Frequent travelers to UAE wanting convenience of pre-approved visa
- Nationalities not eligible for visa-on-arrival
- Travelers wanting longer validity than standard 30/90-day tourist visas
- Business visitors making multiple short trips (without employment)

## UAE - work Visa
### Source: UAE_work.txt

LAST UPDATED: 2024
=== OVERVIEW ===
- 5-year renewable residence visa that allows holder to sponsor themselves
- No requirement for UAE national or employer sponsorship
- Eligible categories: Freelancers/self-employed individuals, skilled employees

---CHUNK:739---
cers/self-employed individuals, skilled employees
- Provides greater flexibility and stability compared to standard employer-sponsored visas
- Holders can sponsor family members (subject to standard family sponsorship requirements)

ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA:
□ Hold valid freelance/self-employment permit from Ministry of Human Resources and Emiratisation (MOHRE)
□ Hold bachelor's degree OR specialized diploma relevant to freelance activity
□ Provide ONE of the following financial proofs:

---CHUNK:740---
□ Provide ONE of the following financial proofs:
- Evidence of annual income from self-employment ≥ AED 360,000 for each of previous two years, OR
- Proof of financial solvency throughout intended stay in UAE

- Apply via MOHRE Freelance Portal: https://www.mohre.gov.ae/freelance
- Eligible activities: Media, marketing, consulting, education, technology, design, arts, etc.

---CHUNK:741---
on activity and emirate

- Client contracts/invoices demonstrating project revenue
- Tax returns from UAE or home country (converted to AED)
- Average calculation: AED 30,000/month over 24 months
SOLVENCY-BASED (ALTERNATIVE TO INCOME THRESHOLD):
- Bank statements (last 12 months) showing balance ≥ AED 300,000
- Investment portfolio statements valued ≥ AED 500,000

estment portfolio statements valued ≥ AED 500,000

ADVANTAGES OVER STANDARD VISA:
- Green Visa validity (5 years) provides longer stability for sponsored dependents
- No employer dependency: Family visas not affected if Green Visa holder changes jobs or becomes unemployed (as long as Green Visa remains valid)

- Freelancers: Must maintain valid MOHRE freelance permit AND continue to meet income/solvency requirements

---CHUNK:755---
AND continue to meet income/solvency requirements
- Skilled employees: Must maintain qualifying employment OR secure new qualifying job within 6 months of previous employment ending
- No criminal record or immigration violations during visa validity
- Valid passport (6+ months remaining at renewal application)
RENEWAL STEPS:
1. Submit renewal application via ICP/GDRFA portal 30-90 days before expiry
2. Provide updated supporting documents:
- Freelancers: Renewed freelance permit, updated income/financial proof

---CHUNK:756---
freelance permit, updated income/financial proof
- Skilled employees: New/continued employment contract, updated salary proof, MOHRE occupational confirmation
3. Complete medical examination if required (typically every 5 years)
4. Pay renewal fees (similar structure to initial issuance)
5. Receive renewed Green Visa + updated Emirates ID
=== VISA CANCELLATION CONDITIONS ===
GREEN VISA MAY BE CANCELLED IF:
✗ Freelancer: Loses MOHRE freelance permit OR income falls below threshold for 2 consecutive years

---CHUNK:757---
ome falls below threshold for 2 consecutive years
✗ Skilled employee: Employment contract terminated AND no new qualifying job secured within 6-month grace period
✗ Holder convicted of serious crime or poses security threat to UAE
✗ Fraudulent documents or misrepresentation discovered during validity period
✗ Holder abandons UAE residency (stays outside UAE >6 months continuously without valid reason)
✗ Violation of UAE laws or immigration regulations
GRACE PERIOD FOR JOB LOSS (SKILLED EMPLOYEES ONLY):

---CHUNK:758---
ACE PERIOD FOR JOB LOSS (SKILLED EMPLOYEES ONLY):
- If employment ends: 6-month grace period to secure new qualifying job
- During grace period: Green Visa remains valid; holder can stay in UAE, sponsor family, seek new employment
- If no new job secured within 6 months: Visa may be cancelled; dependent visas affected simultaneously
CONSEQUENCES OF CANCELLATION:
- 30-day grace period to either rectify status or depart UAE
- Sponsored dependents' visas cancelled simultaneously

---CHUNK:759---
nsored dependents' visas cancelled simultaneously

- Potential fines or penalties depending on violation nature
=== TRANSITION FROM STANDARD WORK VISA ===
ELIGIBILITY TO SWITCH:
- Holders of standard employer-sponsored work visa CAN apply for Green Visa if they meet eligibility criteria
- No requirement to leave UAE; application can be submitted from within country
PROCESS:
1.

---CHUNK:760---
can be submitted from within country
PROCESS:
1. Ensure eligibility: Freelancers obtain MOHRE permit; skilled employees verify occupational level/salary
2. Submit Green Visa application via ICP/GDRFA portal while holding standard visa
3. If approved: Standard visa cancelled; Green Visa issued (no gap in legal status)
4. Notify current employer of status change (if remaining with same employer)
ADVANTAGES OF SWITCHING:
- Independence from employer sponsorship
- Longer validity (5 years vs. 2 years standard)

---CHUNK:761---
- Longer validity (5 years vs. 2 years standard)

ency) | Low (requires new employer sponsorship) |

| Application | Individual applies directly | Employer applies on behalf of employee |

## UK - family Visa
### Source: UK_family.txt
VISA TYPE: Family Visa (Partner/Spouse Route)
COUNTRY: United Kingdom
SOURCE: https://www.gov.uk/uk-family-visa
LAST UPDATED: 2024
=== OVERVIEW ===
You need a family visa to live with a family member in the UK for more than 6 months.

---CHUNK:768---
a family member in the UK for more than 6 months.
Eligible relationships: spouse, partner, fiancé(e), child, parent, relative providing long-term care.
=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA - PARTNER ROUTE ===
APPLICANT AND PARTNER MUST:
- Both be 18 or over
- Intend to live together permanently in the UK after application
- Partner must be: British/Irish citizen OR settled in UK (ILR, settled status) OR pre-settled status (EU/EEA/Swiss, arrived before 1 Jan 2021) OR have Turkish Businessperson/Worker visa OR refugee/humanitarian protection OR stateless

---CHUNK:769---
a OR refugee/humanitarian protection OR stateless person leave

- Marriage or civil partnership recognized in UK
- Living together in relationship for at least 2 years at time of application
- Fiancé(e)/proposed civil partner planning to marry/enter civil partnership in UK within 6 months of arrival
- In relationship 2+ years but cannot live together due to work/study/cultural reasons (provide evidence of ongoing commitment)
=== FINANCIAL REQUIREMENTS ===
MINIMUM INCOME THRESHOLD:

---CHUNK:770---
ANCIAL REQUIREMENTS ===
MINIMUM INCOME THRESHOLD:
- Standard: £29,000 combined annual income (applicant + partner)
- Transitional protection (applied as partner before 11 April 2024): £18,600 combined income
- Additional for children: £3,800 for first child, £2,400 for each additional child (capped at £29,000 total)
EXEMPTIONS FROM MINIMUM INCOME:
- Partner receives qualifying disability/carer benefits: Disability Living Allowance, PIP, Attendance Allowance, Carer's Allowance, Armed Forces Independence Payment, etc.

---CHUNK:771---
llowance, Armed Forces Independence Payment, etc.
- Human rights claim: Child in UK who is British/Irish or lived 7+ years in UK, and unreasonable for child to leave
- Human rights breach: Refusal would breach applicant's human rights
PROOF OF INCOME:
- Employment: Payslips (6 months), employer letter, bank statements
- Self-employment: Tax returns, accounts, dividend vouchers
- Savings: £16,000+ held for 6 months (can supplement income shortfall)
- Pension, benefits, or other specified sources
=== ENGLISH LANGUAGE REQUIREMENT ===

---CHUNK:772---
fied sources
=== ENGLISH LANGUAGE REQUIREMENT ===
MUST PROVE ENGLISH AT CEFR LEVEL A1 (SPEAKING & LISTENING) VIA:
- Approved SELT test (IELTS Life Skills A1, Trinity GESE Grade 2, etc.)
- Academic qualification taught in English recognized as equivalent to UK degree
- National of majority English-speaking country (USA, Canada, Australia, New Zealand, etc.)
=== DOCUMENTS REQUIRED ===

---CHUNK:773---

=== FEES & COSTS ===

---CHUNK:774---

- Outside UK: £1,938 (joining partner/parent/child)
- Inside UK: £1,321 (joining partner/parent/child)

- Adult dependent relative (care): £3,413 (outside UK) / £1,321 (inside UK) OR £424/£1,321 if sponsor has refugee/humanitarian protection

- Adults (18+): £2,587.50 (2.5 years), £3,105 (2.75 years), £5,175 (5 years)

=== PROCESSING TIMES ===
- Outside UK: Usually 12 weeks
- Inside UK (meeting all requirements): Usually 8 weeks
- Inside UK (not meeting financial/English requirements): ~12 months
=== DURATION & EXTENSION ===
- Initial grant: 2 years 9 months (partner route) or 6 months (fiancé(e) route)

---CHUNK:776---
ths (partner route) or 6 months (fiancé(e) route)
- Extension: Apply before current visa expires; grants additional 2 years 6 months
- Can extend multiple times
=== SETTLEMENT (INDEFINITE LEAVE TO REMAIN) ===
- Earliest eligibility: After 5 years continuous residence in UK on family visa as partner
- Time spent as fiancé(e) does NOT count toward 5 years
- Time spent on other visas does NOT count
- Must still meet financial and English requirements at settlement stage (unless exempt)
=== SWITCHING RULES ===

---CHUNK:777---
ent stage (unless exempt)
=== SWITCHING RULES ===
CAN SWITCH TO FAMILY VISA FROM INSIDE UK IF:
- Currently on: Most work visas, student visas, graduate visa, certain humanitarian protections
- Applying to stay with same eligible partner/family member
CANNOT SWITCH FROM INSIDE UK IF:
- Currently on: Standard Visitor visa, visa for 6 months or less
- Family member is in UK temporarily on work/student visa (apply as dependant instead)
=== EXCLUSION CRITERIA (WHEN YOU CANNOT APPLY) ===

---CHUNK:778---
== EXCLUSION CRITERIA (WHEN YOU CANNOT APPLY) ===
✗ Family member has only temporary work/student visa (apply as dependant instead)
✗ Applicant has visitor visa or permission for ≤6 months (usually must leave UK to apply)
✗ Relationship is not genuine/subsisting or entered for immigration purposes
✗ General grounds for refusal apply (criminal history, deception, unpaid NHS debts, etc.)
=== SPECIAL CIRCUMSTANCES ===
DOMESTIC ABUSE OR PARTNER DEATH:
- May apply to settle in UK if permission was as partner and:

---CHUNK:779---
to settle in UK if permission was as partner and:
- Applicant was victim of domestic abuse, OR
- Partner died during relationship
- Must provide evidence (police reports, court orders, death certificate, support letters)
PRIVATE LIFE ROUTE (ALTERNATIVE PATH):
- Under 18 + lived in UK continuously 7+ years + unreasonable to leave
- Age 18-24 + lived in UK > half your life
- 18+ + <20 years in UK + very significant problems returning to home country
- 20+ years continuous residence in UK

---CHUNK:780---
me country
- 20+ years continuous residence in UK
- Grants 2.5 years initially; settlement after 5 or 10 years depending on category

## UK - work Visa
### Source: UK_work.txt
VISA TYPE: Skilled Worker Visa (Work)
COUNTRY: United Kingdom
SOURCE: https://www.gov.uk/skilled-worker-visa/eligibility
LAST UPDATED: 2024
=== ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA ===
Your job:
- Work for a UK employer that's been approved by the Home Office

---CHUNK:781---
employer that's been approved by the Home Office
- Have a 'certificate of sponsorship' (CoS) from your employer with information about the role you've been offered in the UK
- Do a job that's on the list of eligible occupations
- Be paid a minimum salary - how much depends on the type of work you do and the date you got your CoS
- Must have a confirmed job offer before you apply for your visa
Knowledge of English:
- Must be able to speak, read, write and understand English
- Usually need to prove knowledge of English when you apply

---CHUNK:782---
need to prove knowledge of English when you apply
=== POINTS-BASED SYSTEM (Must score 70 points total) ===
- 50 points: Mandatory criteria (job offer from approved sponsor, job at appropriate skill level, English at B1)
- 20 points: Salary criteria (meet general threshold OR going rate for occupation OR new entrant rate)
=== SALARY THRESHOLDS (2024) ===
- General threshold: £38,700 per year OR the "going rate" for your occupation code (whichever is higher)
- Health/education workers: £30,960 per year OR going rate

---CHUNK:783---
education workers: £30,960 per year OR going rate
- New entrants (under 26, recent graduate, switching from Student visa): 70% of going rate OR £30,960 (whichever is higher)
=== ENGLISH LANGUAGE PROOF OPTIONS ===
- Pass an approved SELT test at CEFR level B1 (reading, writing, speaking, listening)
- Have an academic qualification taught in English equivalent to UK bachelor's/master's/PhD
- Be a national of a majority English-speaking country (USA, Canada, Australia, New Zealand, etc.)
=== MAINTENANCE FUNDS ===

---CHUNK:784---
lia, New Zealand, etc.)
=== MAINTENANCE FUNDS ===
- Must have £1,270 in bank account for 28 consecutive days before applying
- OR sponsor certifies maintenance on CoS (exempts this requirement)
=== DOCUMENTS REQUIRED ===
- Certificate of sponsorship reference number (from employer)
- Proof of English knowledge
- Valid passport or identity document
- Job title and annual salary
- Job's occupation code
- Employer name and sponsor licence number (on CoS)
- TB test certificate (if from listed country)

---CHUNK:785---
S)
- TB test certificate (if from listed country)
- Criminal record certificate (for education/healthcare roles)
=== FEES & PROCESSING ===
- Application fee: £719–£1,420 (depends on duration and shortage occupation)
- Immigration Health Surcharge: £1,035 per year
- Standard processing: 3 weeks (outside UK), 8 weeks (inside UK)
=== SWITCHING RULES ===
- Can apply from inside UK if on: Student visa, Graduate visa, certain work visas
- Must apply from outside UK if on: Visitor visa, short-term study visa

- Must demonstrate ability to financially support the beneficiary (Form I-864, Affidavit of Support)
- Must provide proof of relationship (marriage certificate, birth certificate, adoption decree)
ELIGIBILITY CRITERIA - BENEFICIARY (APPLICANT):
- Must prove bona fide relationship (not entered for immigration purposes only)

F1: Unmarried sons and daughters (21+) of U.S. citizens
F2A: Spouses and unmarried children (under 21) of Lawful Permanent Residents
F2B: Unmarried sons and daughters (21+) of Lawful Permanent Residents

and daughters (21+) of Lawful Permanent Residents

- Must not have violated prior U.S. immigration laws (unlawful presence, fraud, etc.)
